There are four players in two fixed partnerships. Partners sit facing each other. A standard 52 card pack is used. The cards in each suit rank from highest to lowest: A K Q J 10 9 8 7 6 5 4 3 2.\r\n\r\nThe player to the dealer's left leads to the first trick. Any card may be led.
